#耶律何魯掃古, courtesy name 烏古隣 Wugulin. In 1055 made Langjun. In 1056 安州団練使. Between 1075-1084 made 懐德軍節度使・奚六部禿里太尉. Together with Shumishi he administered Northeastern frontier. He was respected by Daozong. In 1092 made 西北路招討使事. Due to the raid of Yedugua tribe, he invited Northern Zubu under Mogusi to attack them. For his merit was promoted to 左僕射. Once again wanted to attack Yedugua, but by accident he struck at Mogusi's tribe which led to the rebellion by the latter. In 1093 he was sentenced to canning for not reporting the truth about the accident and got stripped of rank. In 1100 became Tigin and Shizhong. In 1103 became 南院大王. Died not soon after.
#石抹明里 - grandson of 石抹曷魯, 石抹宜孫 - 迪烈乣人, 石抹也先 -

In 9th month of 988 led a vanguard force against Northern Song and struck Dingzhou 定州, where he defeated Li Zhongji 李忠吉. For that he was promoted again to 東京統軍使 and 加金紫崇禄大夫. In 7th month of 995 along with Prince of Xi 和朔奴 he attacked Wure 兀惹, but was defeated. Lost for that his 削金紫崇禄大夫阶. In 7th month of 1001 became 拜南府宰相. In 1003 once again invaded Song and in battle of Wangdu took Wang Jizhong prisoner. 功加同政事门下平章事. In 1008 made a Jiedushi of Liaoxing 遼興軍節度使. And later once again made 南府宰相. In 1012 died.

1413932 = { #蕭貴哥 Xiao Guige, 元妃 Consort Yuan. 17 years old when she became a consort.
